<p><b>Jordi Alba Ramos</b> (born 21 March 1989) is a Spanish professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Defender_(association_football)#Full-back" title="Defender (association football)">left-back</a> for <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team" title="Spain national football team">Spain national team</a>.
</p><p>Alba started his career at Barcelona, but was released after being deemed too small. After joining <a href="/wiki/UE_Cornell%C3%A0" title="UE Cornellà">Cornellà</a>, he moved to <a href="/wiki/Valencia_CF" title="Valencia CF">Valencia</a>. In 2012 he returned to Barcelona, with whom he went on to win 14 major honours, including five La Liga titles, four <a href="/wiki/Copa_del_Rey" title="Copa del Rey">Copas del Rey</a> and one <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a>.
</p><p>After winning 23 caps and scoring one goal at youth level, Alba made his senior debut for Spain in 2011. He was an integral member of the team that won <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012" title="UEFA Euro 2012">UEFA Euro 2012</a>, and was also part of the squads at the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014</a> and <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cups</a> and <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016" title="UEFA Euro 2016">Euro 2016</a>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Jordi_Alba&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Club career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_years">Early years</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Jordi_Alba&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Early years">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Alba was born in <a href="/wiki/L%27Hospitalet_de_Llobregat" title="L&#39;Hospitalet de Llobregat">L'Hospitalet de Llobregat</a>, <a href="/wiki/Province_of_Barcelona" title="Province of Barcelona">Barcelona</a>, <a href="/wiki/Catalonia" title="Catalonia">Catalonia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> He started his career in the <a href="/wiki/La_Masia" title="La Masia">youth ranks</a> of <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a> as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Winger" title="Midfielder">left winger</a>, but was released by the club in 2005 for being too small.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> He then joined neighbouring club <a href="/wiki/UE_Cornell%C3%A0" title="UE Cornellà">Cornellà</a> and, after almost two years, departed in a €6,000 transfer to <a href="/wiki/Valencia_CF" title="Valencia CF">Valencia</a> where he finished his football education.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After helping <a href="/wiki/Valencia_CF_Mestalla" title="Valencia CF Mestalla">the reserves</a> earn promotion from <a href="/wiki/Tercera_Divisi%C3%B3n" title="Tercera División">Tercera División</a> in <a href="/wiki/2007%E2%80%9308_Tercera_Divisi%C3%B3n#Grupo_VI" title="2007–08 Tercera División">2007–08</a>, Alba played on loan at <a href="/wiki/Segunda_Divisi%C3%B3n" title="Segunda División">Segunda División</a> club <a href="/wiki/Gimn%C3%A0stic_de_Tarragona" title="Gimnàstic de Tarragona">Gimnàstic de Tarragona</a> <a href="/wiki/2008%E2%80%9309_Segunda_Divisi%C3%B3n" title="2008–09 Segunda División">the following season</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> where he made 22 starts.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (November 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Valencia">Valencia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Jordi_Alba&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Valencia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Jordi_Alba.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d8/Jordi_Alba.jpg/170px-Jordi_Alba.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="260" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d8/Jordi_Alba.jpg/255px-Jordi_Alba.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d8/Jordi_Alba.jpg/340px-Jordi_Alba.jpg 2x" data-file-width="508" data-file-height="778" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Jordi_Alba.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Alba playing for <a href="/wiki/Valencia_CF" title="Valencia CF">Valencia</a> in 2011</div></div></div>
<p>After returning to <i>Los Che</i>, Alba made his <a href="/wiki/La_Liga" title="La Liga">La Liga</a> debut on 13 September 2009, in a 4–2 win at <a href="/wiki/Real_Valladolid" title="Real Valladolid">Real Valladolid</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> He then started in two consecutive <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Europa_League" title="UEFA Europa League">UEFA Europa League</a> <a href="/wiki/2009%E2%80%9310_UEFA_Europa_League" title="2009–10 UEFA Europa League">group stage matches</a>, against <a href="/wiki/Lille_OSC" title="Lille OSC">Lille</a> and <a href="/wiki/SK_Slavia_Prague" title="SK Slavia Prague">Slavia Prague</a> (both 1–1 draws, respectively away and home).<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> Due to continuing injuries in Valencia's defence, he played much of <a href="/wiki/2009%E2%80%9310_La_Liga" title="2009–10 La Liga">2009–10</a> as a <a href="/wiki/Defender_(association_football)#Full-back" title="Defender (association football)">left back</a>, posting overall good performances. In that position, on 11 April 2010, he scored his first goal for the club, in a 2–3 away loss to <a href="/wiki/RCD_Mallorca" title="RCD Mallorca">Mallorca</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_La_Liga" title="2010–11 La Liga">2010–11</a>, still with <a href="/wiki/Unai_Emery" title="Unai Emery">Unai Emery</a> in charge, Alba was used almost always as a defender, battling for first-choice status with <a href="/wiki/J%C3%A9r%C3%A9my_Mathieu" title="Jérémy Mathieu">Jérémy Mathieu</a>. He made 27 league appearances as the team again finished third, subsequently qualifying for the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (November 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_La_Liga" title="2011–12 La Liga">the following campaign</a>, Emery began using both players on Valencia's left side, a strategy he had tested the previous season.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> This proved an effective tactic as Alba and Mathieu frequently interchanged position and offered support for one another in both attacking and defensive areas;<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> ultimately, the player credited the manager as a "key man" in his successful transition to a more defensive role.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Barcelona">Barcelona</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Jordi_Alba&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Barcelona">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On 22 June 2012, Alba signed a five-year contract with Barcelona for a transfer fee of €14&#160;million.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> He made his official debut on 19 August, playing the full 90 minutes in a 5–1 home win against <a href="/wiki/Real_Sociedad" title="Real Sociedad">Real Sociedad</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Alba scored his first goal for the <i>Blaugrana</i> on 20 October 2012, the opener in a 5–4 win at <a href="/wiki/Deportivo_de_La_Coru%C3%B1a" title="Deportivo de La Coruña">Deportivo La Coruña</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> and scoring an <a href="/wiki/Own_goal" title="Own goal">own goal</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> In the following game, at home against <a href="/wiki/Celtic_F.C." title="Celtic F.C.">Celtic</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2012–13 UEFA Champions League">Champions League group stage</a>, he found the net in the <a href="/wiki/Last-minute_goal" title="Last-minute goal">93rd minute</a> of a 2–1 win.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 12 March 2013, Alba scored his fifth goal of the campaign, scoring in the <a href="/wiki/Last-minute_goal" title="Last-minute goal">last minute</a> to complete Barcelona's 4–0 home win over <a href="/wiki/A.C._Milan" title="A.C. Milan">A.C. Milan</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2012-13_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_phase" class="mw-redirect" title="2012-13 UEFA Champions League knockout phase">Champions League round of 16</a> after a 0–2 first leg defeat at the <a href="/wiki/San_Siro" title="San Siro">San Siro</a>, when his team was the first in the competition's history to overturn such a deficit.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> He ended <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_FC_Barcelona_season" title="2012–13 FC Barcelona season">his first season</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Camp_Nou" title="Camp Nou">Camp Nou</a> as <a href="/wiki/List_of_Spanish_football_champions" title="List of Spanish football champions">league champion</a>, as <a href="/wiki/Tito_Vilanova" title="Tito Vilanova">Tito Vilanova</a>'s side regained the title from <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_C.F." class="mw-redirect" title="Real Madrid C.F.">Real Madrid</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 2 June 2015, Alba agreed to a new five-year contract with a new buyout clause of €150&#160;million.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> Four days later, he started in the <a href="/wiki/2015_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2015 UEFA Champions League Final">Champions League final</a>, helping the club to its fifth win in the competition by beating <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a> 3-1 at <a href="/wiki/Berlin" title="Berlin">Berlin</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Olympiastadion_(Berlin)" title="Olympiastadion (Berlin)">Olympiastadion</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> He made 38 appearances in all competitions, with one goal,<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>) as Barça won a <a href="/wiki/Treble_(association_football)" title="Treble (association football)">treble</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Triple_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Triple-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 22 May 2016, Alba won the second <a href="/wiki/Copa_del_Rey" title="Copa del Rey">Copa del Rey</a> of his career, scoring in the 97th minute of <a href="/wiki/2016_Copa_del_Rey_Final" title="2016 Copa del Rey Final">the final</a> against <a href="/wiki/Sevilla_FC" title="Sevilla FC">Sevilla</a> after a through pass from <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a>, in an eventual 2–0 <a href="/wiki/Overtime_(sports)" title="Overtime (sports)">extra time</a> win at the <a href="/wiki/Vicente_Calder%C3%B3n_Stadium" title="Vicente Calderón Stadium">Vicente Calderón</a> in <a href="/wiki/Madrid" title="Madrid">Madrid</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Alba missed out on 50% of the games in the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_FC_Barcelona_season" title="2019–20 FC Barcelona season">2019-20 season</a>, missing 12 out of 24 games, due to a <a href="/wiki/Hamstring_injury" class="mw-redirect" title="Hamstring injury">hamstring injury</a> and a muscle injury.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 11 March 2019, Alba agreed to a new five-year contract with a new buyout clause of €500&#160;million.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Jordi_Alba&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: International career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Jordi_Alba_goal_celebration_Euro_2012_final.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/Jordi_Alba_goal_celebration_Euro_2012_final.jpg/250px-Jordi_Alba_goal_celebration_Euro_2012_final.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="166" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/Jordi_Alba_goal_celebration_Euro_2012_final.jpg/375px-Jordi_Alba_goal_celebration_Euro_2012_final.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/89/Jordi_Alba_goal_celebration_Euro_2012_final.jpg/500px-Jordi_Alba_goal_celebration_Euro_2012_final.jpg 2x" data-file-width="656" data-file-height="435" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Jordi_Alba_goal_celebration_Euro_2012_final.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Alba <a href="/wiki/Goal_celebration" title="Goal celebration">celebrating his goal</a> for <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team" title="Spain national football team">Spain</a> in the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012_Final" title="UEFA Euro 2012 Final">UEFA Euro 2012 Final</a></div></div></div>
<p>Alba represented <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_under-19_football_team" title="Spain national under-19 football team">Spain</a> at the <a href="/wiki/2008_UEFA_European_Under-19_Championship" title="2008 UEFA European Under-19 Championship">2008 UEFA European Under-19 Championship</a>, as well as appearing in all four games as the country won the <a href="/wiki/Gold_medal" title="Gold medal">gold medal</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Football_at_the_2009_Mediterranean_Games" title="Football at the 2009 Mediterranean Games">2009 Mediterranenan Games</a>. He was also part of the squad at the <a href="/wiki/2009_FIFA_U-20_World_Cup" title="2009 FIFA U-20 World Cup">2009 FIFA U-20 World Cup</a> in <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2020)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>
</p><p>Alba received his first call-up to the <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team" title="Spain national football team">full national team</a> on 30 September 2011, for the last two <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012" title="UEFA Euro 2012">UEFA Euro 2012</a> <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012_qualifying" title="UEFA Euro 2012 qualifying">qualifiers</a> against the <a href="/wiki/Czech_Republic_national_football_team" title="Czech Republic national football team">Czech Republic</a> and <a href="/wiki/Scotland_national_football_team" title="Scotland national football team">Scotland</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> He made his debut against Scotland on 11 October, a 3–1 win in <a href="/wiki/Alicante" title="Alicante">Alicante</a> in which his cut back from the left wing provided the <a href="/wiki/Assist_(football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Assist (football)">assist</a> for the opening goal, scored by former Valencia teammate <a href="/wiki/David_Silva" title="David Silva">David Silva</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> His impressive debut confirmed his status as a strong candidate to be the long-term successor of <a href="/wiki/Joan_Capdevila" title="Joan Capdevila">Joan Capdevila</a> as the regular left back for <i>La Roja</i>,<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> and he was also included in the <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_under-23_football_team" title="Spain national under-23 football team">under-23 squad</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2012_Summer_Olympics" title="2012 Summer Olympics">2012 Summer Olympics</a> in <a href="/wiki/London" title="London">London</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Alba was included in <a href="/wiki/Vicente_del_Bosque" title="Vicente del Bosque">Vicente del Bosque</a>'s squad for the Euro 2012 finals in Poland and Ukraine, and played in every match, as Spain won the tournament. He supplied the cross for <a href="/wiki/Xabi_Alonso" title="Xabi Alonso">Xabi Alonso</a> to open the scoring in the 2–0 quarter-final victory over <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">France</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> In <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012_Final" title="UEFA Euro 2012 Final">the final</a> against <a href="/wiki/Italy_national_football_team" title="Italy national football team">Italy</a>, after running onto a pass from <a href="/wiki/Xavi" title="Xavi">Xavi</a> during a counter-attack, he scored the second goal in a 4–0 win.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Alba was also selected for the <a href="/wiki/2013_FIFA_Confederations_Cup" title="2013 FIFA Confederations Cup">2013 FIFA Confederations Cup</a> in Brazil. He played four complete matches during the tournament, scoring twice in the 3–0 group stage win over <a href="/wiki/Nigeria_national_football_team" title="Nigeria national football team">Nigeria</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Alba made Del Bosque's squad for the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</a> in <a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> making three appearances as the defending champions were knocked out in the group stage.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> He was also named in <a href="/wiki/Julen_Lopetegui" title="Julen Lopetegui">Julen Lopetegui</a>'s squad for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 World Cup</a> in <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Jordi_Alba&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Style of play">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Alba is a diminutive, technically gifted, mobile, and fast attacking <a href="/wiki/Defender_(association_football)#Full-back" title="Defender (association football)">left-back</a>, who can also be used as a <a href="/wiki/Left_winger" class="mw-redirect" title="Left winger">left winger</a>; he is known for his link-up play, positioning, movement, and his ability to time his attacking runs into space and get up the flank, as well as his ability deliver <a href="/wiki/Cross_(football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Cross (football)">crosses</a> into the box, which allows him to provide assists for teammates. Moreover, he is also a tenacious tackler; however, his defending has been cited as a weakness by certain pundits, such as Enrique Ortego of <i><a href="/wiki/Marca_(newspaper)" title="Marca (newspaper)">Marca</a></i>, although he was able to improve upon this aspect of his game as his career progressed.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-A_closer_look_at_Spain’s_Euro_2012_squad_42-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-A_closer_look_at_Spain’s_Euro_2012_squad-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Fullback_Alba_giving_Spain_added_goalscoring_value_43-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fullback_Alba_giving_Spain_added_goalscoring_value-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Top_10_Left-Backs_in_World_46-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Top_10_Left-Backs_in_World-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> His pace and stamina allows him to be very involved in both his team's offensive and defensive plays, as he can get from one end of the pitch to the other very quickly, often pushing forward to get past players and score goals, or falling back when his team have lost possession.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> Regarded as one of the best left-backs in the world in the media,<sup id="cite_ref-Top_10_Left-Backs_in_World_46-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Top_10_Left-Backs_in_World-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> Alba has earned plaudits from former left-backs Joan Capdevila and <a href="/wiki/Roberto_Carlos" title="Roberto Carlos">Roberto Carlos</a> over his playing style and ability.<sup id="cite_ref-Fullback_Alba_giving_Spain_added_goalscoring_value_43-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Fullback_Alba_giving_Spain_added_goalscoring_value-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_statistics">Career statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Jordi_Alba&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Career statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Club">Club</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Jordi_Alba&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Club">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
